   var requestAnimationFrame = window.requestAnimationFrame || window.mozRequestAnimationFrame || window.webkitRequestAnimationFrame || window.msRequestAnimationFrame;
   var deferredCssElement = document.getElementById('deferred-css');
   var cssLoadListeners = [];
   var isCssLoaded;
 
   if (deferredCssElement === null) {
     isCssLoaded = true;
   } else {
     isCssLoaded = false;
 
     document.body.addEventListener('load', handleLoadEvent, true);
 
     if (requestAnimationFrame) {
       requestAnimationFrame(function () {
         window.setTimeout(loadDeferredCss, 0);
       });
     } else {
       window.addEventListener('load', loadDeferredCss);
     }
   }
 
   window.addCssLoadEventListener = function (listener) {
     if (isCssLoaded) {
       listener();
     } else {
       cssLoadListeners.push(listener);
     }
   };
 
   function loadDeferredCss() {
     var divElement = document.createElement('div');
 
     if (deferredCssElement) {
       divElement.innerHTML = deferredCssElement.textContent;
       document.body.appendChild(divElement);
       deferredCssElement.parentElement.removeChild(deferredCssElement);
     }
   }
 
   function handleLoadEvent(event) {
     var preLoaderCssElement;
 
     if (event && event.target && event.target.className === 'css') {
       isCssLoaded = true;
 
       preLoaderCssElement = document.getElementById('preloader-css');
       if (preLoaderCssElement !== null) {
         preLoaderCssElement.parentNode.removeChild(preLoaderCssElement);
       }
 
       cssLoadListeners.forEach(function (listener) {
         listener();
       });
     }
   }
 }());

   function createRegexVendorMap(vendorMap) {
     var mapWithRegexes = {};
     for (var libraryName in vendorMap) {
       if (!vendorMap.hasOwnProperty(libraryName)) {
         continue;
       }
       mapWithRegexes[['vendor', libraryName].join('/')] = {
         'versioned': vendorMap[libraryName],
         'regexp': new RegExp('^vendor/' + libraryName + '/')
       };
     }
     return mapWithRegexes;
   }
 
   function getVersioned(input, mapWithRegexes) {
     var regexp, versioned, source;
     for (source in mapWithRegexes) {
       if (!mapWithRegexes.hasOwnProperty(source)) {
         continue;
       }
       regexp = mapWithRegexes[source].regexp;
       if (!input.match(regexp)) {
         continue;
       }
       versioned = mapWithRegexes[source].versioned + '/';
       return input.replace(regexp, versioned);
     }
     return input;
   }
 
   function mapPaths(paths) {

       if (!mapWithRegexes.hasOwnProperty(libraryName)) {
         continue;
       }
       mappedPaths[libraryName] = mapWithRegexes[libraryName].versioned;
     }
     return mappedPaths;

          <section class="inner">
           <div class="row-fluid" data-last-row-on-mobile="true">
            <div class="text span12" style="">
             <div class="textInner">
              <h2 style="text-align: center;">
               Motorline Group was founded in 1972
              </h2>
              <h1 style="text-align: center;">
               Welcome to Motorline Group
              </h1>
              <p>
               <br/>
              </p>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="row-fluid">
            <div class="text span4">
             <div class="textInner">
              <p>
               The
               <strong>
                Motorline Group
               </strong>
               is a thriving family business, with dealerships across
               <strong>
                Kent, West Sussex, Surrey, Reading, Wales, Oxford, Bristol and Midlands.
               </strong>
               <strong>
                <strong>
                </strong>
               </strong>
              </p>
              <p>
               <strong>
                <strong>
                </strong>
               </strong>
              </p>
              <p>
               <strong>
                Across our network of showrooms, we stock vehicles from quality carmakers 
               </strong>
               Toyota, Nissan, Volkswagen, Renault, Peugeot, Skoda, Lexus, Maserati, Infiniti and Dacia. We provide top-quality, brand-new and Approved Used cars, along with excellent aftersales services. We have locations in
               <strong>
                Ashford, Canterbury, Crawley, Dartford, Horsham, Maidstone, Tunbridge Wells, Medway, Coulsdon, Bristol, Newport, Cardiff, Reading, Oxford, Gloucester, Worcester, Hereford, Bromsgrove and Stourbridge.
               </strong>
               <strong>
                <strong>
                </strong>
               </strong>
              </p>
              <p>
               <strong>
                <strong>
                </strong>
               </strong>
              </p>
              <p>
               <br/>
              </p>
             </div>
            </div>
            <div class="text span4">
             <div class="textInner">
              <p>
               <strong>
                The Motorline Group prides itself on offering outstanding
               </strong>
               levels of service to new and existing customers alike. We can deliver advice on your next new or used car purchase, including flexible finance packages to suit your budget. Dont forget to ask about our special offers to get even more value for your money.
              </p>
              <p>
               Our complete aftersales care includes routine
               <strong>
                servicing, MOT, repairs, parts
               </strong>
               and warranty requirements. Our in-house, manufacturer-trained technicians are highly trained to deliver exceptional services  every single time. Whats more, when you come to us for repairs we you will only receive the absolute best. We only use manufacturer-approved, genuine parts. Its all part of our commitment to the highest quality in everything we do.
              </p>
              <p>
               <br/>
              </p>
             </div>
            </div>
            <div class="text span4">
             <div class="textInner">
              <p>
               The Motorline Group is also a member of the Motability scheme, which is designed to help disabled people and their carers remain mobile. If youre eligible, talk to us and we can discuss all your options. A wide selection of brands and models are available  plus a range of limited-time offers on certain products and services.
              </p>
              <p>
               Follow the links below to find out more about our dealerships and the services we provide. Our friendly team is on hand to take your call if you want to speak to us directly. Alternatively, you can reach us online and well get back to you as soon as we can.
              </p>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>

         nd.auto.require(["jquery"], function () {
         $("img.css-bg-image").show();
         updateBackgroundImages();
         window.onresize = function(event) { updateBackgroundImages(); };
 
         function updateBackgroundImages() {
             var windowWidth = window.innerWidth || document.documentElement.clientWidth || document.body.clientWidth;
             var device = "desktop";
             if (windowWidth <= 767) device = "mobile";
 
             var backgroundImages = document.querySelectorAll(".css-bg-image");
             for (var i = 0; i < backgroundImages.length; i++) {
                 backgroundImages[i].src = backgroundImages[i].getAttribute("data-" + device + "-src");
             }
         }
         });
